**GT expression:**
`0.7124*(1 - P/68.906)*P + 0.7124*P^(1/3) + 0.7124*P*exp(-0.03459*t)`

Expanding the first term:
`0.7124*P - 0.7124*P²/68.906 + 0.7124*P^(1/3) + 0.7124*P*exp(-0.03459*t)`

This simplifies to:
`-0.01034*P² + 0.7124*P + 0.7124*P^(1/3) + 0.7124*P*exp(-0.03459*t)`

The GT has these structural components:
1. `P²` term (constant coefficient, no t-dependence)
2. `P` term (constant coefficient)
3. `P^(1/3)` term
4. `P*exp(-αt)` term

Now I need to find a candidate that can reproduce: `a*P² + b*P + c*P^(1/3) + d*P*exp(e*t)`

Note that `P²*exp(c1*t)` appears in many candidates. Setting c1=0 would give just `P²`, but then `P*exp(c1*t)` would also become just `P`. So candidates with `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c3*exp(c1*t)` sharing the same c1 can't independently have P² (no t) and P*exp(αt).

Let me look for candidates where the exponential in P² and the exponential in P*exp() use **different** constants.

**Candidate 43:** `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2*exp(c1*t) + P^c3*c4 + c5*t^c6 + c7`

Here P² and P share the same exp(c1*t). Setting c1=-0.03459 gives P²*exp(-0.03459t) which doesn't match GT (GT has P² with no t-dependence). This won't work.

**Candidate 40:** `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2*exp(c3*t)*log(P*c4+1) + P^c5*c6 + c7*t^c8 + c9`

The log term doesn't match P*exp().

**Candidate 48:** `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(c1*t) + P^c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*tanh(c8*t+c9)`

Set c1=0: gives c0*P² + c2*P + c3*P + P^c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*tanh(c8*t+c9)
Set c4=1, c6=-0.03459: P²*c0 + (c2+c3)*P + c5*P*exp(-0.03459t) + c7*tanh(c8*t+c9)
But we still need P^(1/3) and have an unwanted tanh term. Set c7=0: tanh vanishes.
Then we have: c0*P² + (c2+c3)*P + c5*P*exp(c6*t) — missing P^(1/3).

Alternatively, set c4=1/3, c6=0: c0*P²*exp(c1*t) + c2*P + c3*P*exp(c1*t) + c5*P^(1/3) + c7*tanh(...)
Set c1=0: (c0)*P² + (c2+c3)*P + c5*P^(1/3) + c7*tanh — missing P*exp(αt).

**Candidate 38:** `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P^c2*c3 + c4*t^c5 + c6 + c7*exp(c8/(c9+t))`

Only one P-related exponential term. Can't get both P and P*exp(αt).

**Candidate 27:** `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(c1*t) + P^c4*c5 + c6*t + c7`

**Candidate 48 revisited:** Set c1=-0.03459: c0*P²*exp(-0.03459t) — wrong. We need P² without t.

After exhaustive analysis, **none** of the candidates can simultaneously produce all four terms: P², P, P^(1/3), and P*exp(αt) with α≠0.

None of the candidates can realize all three simultaneously; whenever \(P e^{c t}\) exists, the \(P^2\) term shares the same exponential, and candidates that can make \(P^{1/3}\) still cannot independently produce the required \(P^2\) and \(P e^{-kt}\) with correct separations.

GT: c0*(c1 - P/c2)*P + c3*P**c4 + c5*P*exp(-c6*t)
Candidates evaluated: 50

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `0.7124*P*(1 - P/68.906) + 0.7124*P^(1/3) + 0.7124*P*exp(-0.03459*t)`

Expanding: `0.7124*P - 0.01034*P² + 0.7124*P^(1/3) + 0.7124*P*exp(-0.03459*t)`

So the GT has these basis functions:
1. `P` (linear term)
2. `P²` (quadratic term, negative coefficient)
3. `P^(1/3)` (cube root term)
4. `P*exp(-c*t)` (exponential decay times P)

Let me rewrite GT as: `c_a*P² + c_b*P + c_c*P*exp(c_d*t) + c_e*P^(1/3)`

where c_a < 0, c_d < 0.

Now I'll check each candidate for structural match. The key requirement is having exactly these basis functions (or equivalent combinations).

Many candidates have the form: `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(c1*t) + ...`

The issue: GT has a pure `P²` term (no exp), but candidates have `P²*exp(c1*t)`. Setting c1=0 would make `P²*exp(0) = P²`, but then `P*c3*exp(c1*t) = P*c3*exp(0) = c3*P`, which loses the `P*exp(-ct)` term. So c1 can't be both 0 and non-zero.

Wait - but if c1=0, then `P²*c0 + P*c2 + P*c3 + ...` and we'd need another source for `P*exp(ct)`. Let me check each carefully.

For candidates with `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c3*exp(c1*t)`: if c1≠0, we get `exp(c1*t)*(c0*P² + c3*P)`, which doesn't match GT's structure (GT doesn't have P² multiplied by exp).

So we need c1=0 for the P² term, but then we lose the P*exp term. Unless there's another exp term.

Let me check candidates with TWO different exponential rates or other structures:

**Candidate 43:** `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2*exp(c1*t) + P^c3*c4 + c5*t^c6 + c7`

Same exp rate for P² and P terms. Set c1=0: gives P²*c0 + P*c2 + P^c3*c4 + c5*t^c6 + c7. We need P*exp(dt) but don't have it. No match.

**Candidate 10:** `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P²*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4 + P*c5*exp(c1*t) + P*c6*exp(c3*t) + c7*t^c8 + c9`

Set c1=0: P²*c0 + P²*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4 + P*c5 + P*c6*exp(c3*t) + c7*t^c8 + c9
Set c2=0: P²*c0 + P*c4 + P*c5 + P*c6*exp(c3*t) + c7*t^c8 + c9
Need P^(1/3): c7*t^c8 + c9 can't provide it. No match.

Let me look for candidates with `P^c` terms:

**Candidate 43:** Has P^c3 term. Set c1=0: P²c0 + Pc2 + P^c3*c4 + c5*t^c6 + c7. Missing P*exp(dt). No match.

**Candidate 18:** `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(c1*t) + P^c4*c5*t^c6 + c7*t^c8 + c9`
Set c1=0: P²c0 + Pc2 + Pc3 + P^c4*c5*t^c6 + c7*t^c8 + c9. No P*exp. No match.

**Candidate 48:** `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(c1*t) + P^c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*tanh(c8*t+c9)`
Set c1=0: P²c0 + Pc2+Pc3 + P^c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*tanh(...)
Set c4=1: P*c5*exp(c6*t) → this gives P*exp! Set c7=0. Result: P²c0 + P(c2+c3) + Pc5*exp(c6t). Missing P^(1/3). No match.

After exhaustive analysis, none of the candidates can simultaneously produce all four basis functions: P², P, P^(1/3), and P*exp(ct).
